	JAP_reorganize_the_administrative_apparatus = {
		priority = 1100
		icon = GFX_decision_JAP_reorganize_the_administrative_apparatus
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 150
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): complete decision JAP_reorganize_the_administrative_apparatus"

		}

	JAP_to_issue_the_third_Decree_on_education = {
		priority = 1000
		icon = GFX_decision_JAP_to_issue_the_third_Decree_on_education
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }		
		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = 50 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = JAP_cost_dec }
			check_variable = { has_political_power > custom_cost_pp }
		}
		custom_cost_text = pol_power_cost
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): complete decision JAP_to_issue_the_third_Decree_on_education"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = -50 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = JAP_cost_dec }
				add_political_power = custom_cost_pp
			}
			set_country_flag = JAP_to_issue_the_third_Decree_on_education_flag
			add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_integration_var = 3 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_integration_var_tt }
			JAP_the_level_of_integration = yes
			unlock_decision_tooltip = JAP_to_issue_the_fourth_Decree_on_education
			unlock_decision_tooltip = JAP_decree_on_Civil_Schools
		}
	}

	JAP_actions_of_the_Kwantung_Army_in_Shandong = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		priority = 500
		activation = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = SHA
				597 = { controller = { NOT = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
				743 = { controller = { NOT = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
				has_country_flag = JAP_missions_BLOCK_flag
			}
		} 
		icon = GFX_decision_activate_the_combat_cell_anarchist
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 150
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): timeout mission JAP_actions_of_the_Kwantung_Army_in_Shandong"
			set_country_flag = JAP_actions_of_the_Kwantung_Army_in_Shandong_BLOCK_flag
			country_event = NW_JAP.27
		}
	}

JAP_war_operations = {

	JAP_attack_on_the_USSR = {
		priority = 1500
		icon = border_war
		activation = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				JAP = { NOT = { can_declare_war_on = SOV } }
				POL = { NOT = { can_declare_war_on = SOV } }
				if = {
					limit = { tag = JAP }
					has_war_with = POL
				}
				else = {
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): cancel mission JAP_attack_on_the_USSR"
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no
		war_with_on_timeout = SOV
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): timeout mission JAP_attack_on_the_USSR"
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = JAP }
				declare_war_on = { target = SOV type = topple_government }
				effect_tooltip = { POL = { declare_war_on = { target = SOV type = topple_government } } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = POL }
				declare_war_on = { target = SOV type = topple_government }
				effect_tooltip = { JAP = { declare_war_on = { target = SOV type = topple_government } } }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}

	JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen = {
		priority = 500
		activation = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				if = {
					limit = { original_tag = JAP }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_TEMP = 10 }
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var < JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_TEMP }
						tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_check_tt
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						any_enemy_country = { OR = { is_major = yes original_tag = SOV } }
						NOT = { controls_state = 527 }
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { controls_state = 984 }
						any_enemy_country = { is_major = yes }
						has_civil_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 984
				state = 527
			} 
		}
		icon = border_war
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): timeout mission JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen"
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = JAP }
				start_border_war = {
					change_state_after_war = no
					attacker = {
						state = 527
						num_provinces = 1
						on_win = NW_JAP.36
						on_lose = NW_JAP.37
					}	
					defender = {
						state = 984
						num_provinces = 1
						on_win = NW_JAP.38
						on_lose = NW_JAP.39
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { SOV = { activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = JAP_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled } } }

			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					start_border_war = {
						change_state_after_war = no
						attacker = { state = 527 num_provinces = 1 }	
						defender = { state = 984 num_provinces = 1 }
					}
					activate_targeted_decision = { target = JAP decision = JAP_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }
				}
			}
		}
	}

JAP_operation_Z_category = {
	
	JAP_tora_tora_tora = {
		priority = 950
		activation = { always = no }
		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_subject = yes
				AND = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = USA
							USA = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
						}
						has_war_with = USA
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = HOL
							HOL = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
						}
						has_war_with = HOL
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = event_target:NW_france_scope
							event_target:NW_france_scope = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
						}
						has_war_with = event_target:NW_france_scope
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = PHI
							PHI = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
						}
						has_war_with = PHI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		icon = border_war
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 75
		selectable_mission = no
		war_with_on_timeout = USA
		war_with_on_timeout = HOL
		war_with_on_timeout = PHI
		war_with_on_timeout = FRA
		war_with_on_timeout = FRC
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): timeout mission JAP_tora_tora_tora"
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SIA
					SIA = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
				SIA = { country_event = NW_JAP.122 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = USA
					USA = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = USA type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = HOL
					HOL = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = HOL type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = event_target:NW_france_scope
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = event_target:NW_france_scope type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = PHI
					PHI = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = PHI type = annex_everything }
			}
		}
	}
}

							}

						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						25 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								check_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity < 5 }
							}
							add_to_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = -5 tooltip = JAP_small_parties_popularity_tt }

		priority = 1000
		icon = GFX_decision_activate_the_combat_cell_anarchist

		available = { hidden_trigger = { always = no } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag }
				NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = JAP_holding_positions_mission_tt
					OR = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.is_literally_china
							any_core_state = { controller = { OR = { tag = JAP is_subject_of = JAP is_in_faction_with = JAP } } }
						}
						KOR = { any_core_state = { controller = { OR = { tag = JAP is_subject_of = JAP is_in_faction_with = JAP } } } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): cancel mission JAP_holding_positions_mission (JAP IS COMING BACK)"
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 45
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): timeout mission JAP_holding_positions_mission"
			set_country_flag = JAP_offer_peace_to_Japan_flag
			unlock_decision_tooltip = JAP_offer_peace_to_Japan
		}
	}

		fire_only_once = no

		days_re_enable = 150
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): complete decision JAP_offer_peace_to_Japan"

		}

			base = 0

				add = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = no
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_offer_peace_to_the_chinese_government = {
		priority = 150
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 120
		cost = 10
		available = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
				is_literally_china = yes
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): complete decision JAP_offer_peace_to_the_chinese_government"
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = enemies
						has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china = yes
						has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.315 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = { is_literally_china = yes is_faction_leader = yes has_war_with = ROOT }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.315 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		priority = 50

					has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag
				}

					check_variable = { var = JAP_ugaki_faction_power value = JAP_ugaki_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					tooltip = JAP_ugaki_faction_power_check_tt
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power > 0 }
						check_variable = { JAP_kodoha_faction_power > 0 }
						check_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power > 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power_temp = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power_temp = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_kodoha_faction_power_temp = 1 }

						check_variable = { var = JAP_toseikha_faction_power value = JAP_toseikha_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						tooltip = JAP_toseikha_faction_power_check_tt
					}
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						check_variable = { var = JAP_ugaki_faction_power value = JAP_ugaki_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						tooltip = JAP_ugaki_faction_power_check_tt
					}
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						check_variable = { var = JAP_kodoha_faction_power value = JAP_kodoha_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						tooltip = JAP_kodoha_faction_power_check_tt
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power > 0 }
						check_variable = { JAP_kodoha_faction_power > 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power_temp = 2 }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_kodoha_faction_power_temp = 2 }
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						check_variable = { var = JAP_toseikha_faction_power value = JAP_toseikha_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						tooltip = JAP_toseikha_faction_power_check_tt
					}
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						check_variable = { var = JAP_kodoha_faction_power value = JAP_kodoha_faction_power_temp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						tooltip = JAP_kodoha_faction_power_check_tt
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power > 0 }
						check_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power > 0 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power_temp = 2 }

					}
				}

			JAP_ugaki_office_category_effect = yes

				limit = {

					add_to_variable = { JAP_toseikha_faction_power = -2 tooltip = JAP_toseikha_faction_power_tt }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power > 0 } }
					add_to_variable = { JAP_manchurian_faction_power = 2 tooltip = JAP_manchurian_faction_power_tt }
					add_to_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power = -2 tooltip = JAP_ugaki_faction_power_tt }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_UNLOCK_flag
					has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag

				else_if = {

					}

					add_to_variable = { JAP_kodoha_faction_power = -2 tooltip = JAP_kodoha_faction_power_tt }

				else_if = {

						check_variable = { JAP_ugaki_faction_power > 0 }
					}

	JAP_send_a_group_of_settlers_to_manchukuo = {
		priority = 1000
		icon = JAP_encourage_Koreans_to_join_Japanese_patriotic_organizations
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 250
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = JAP_send_a_group_of_settlers_to_manchukuo_cost_var }
			set_temp_variable = { rifles_temp_cost = 200 }
			check_variable = { var = political_power value = custom_cost_pp compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = num_equipment@infantry_equipment value = rifles_temp_cost compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		custom_cost_text = pol_and_rifles_cost
		cancel_trigger = {
			MAN = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					has_civil_war = yes

					NOT = { controls_state = 761 }
				}
			}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): complete decision JAP_send_a_group_of_settlers_to_manchukuo"

			}
		}

				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_agrarian_expansionism }

			}
			else = {

			}

					50 = { 761 = { add_manpower = JAP_sum_of_manpower } }
				}
				every_core_state = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_japanese_colonists_modifier } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_japanese_colonists_modifier_tt

				add_manpower = -10000
			}
		}

						}
					}

					50 = { 717 = { add_manpower = JAP_sum_of_manpower } }

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse

			set_temp_variable = { custom_cost_pp = 20 }
			check_variable = {
				has_political_power > custom_cost_pp
			} 
			set_temp_variable = { custom_cost_cp = 30 }
			check_variable = {
				has_command_power > custom_cost_cp
			} 
			any_controlled_state = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = fuel_silo
					size > 0
					include_locked = no
				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = slot_and_pol_cost
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: complete decision JAP_give_the_imperial_order_to_observe_military_conventions"
			add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_military_mission days = 30 }
			hidden_effect = {  
				add_political_power = -20 
		
			} 
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = fuel_silo
						size > 0
						include_locked = no
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { add_state_modifier = { modifier = { local_building_slots = -1 } } }
				effect_tooltip = { add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = -1 }
			}
			add_command_power = -30
			add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
			JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
			if = { 
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_3
					add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_2
					add_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1 }
				remove_idea = JAP_problem_with_discipline_idea_1
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 10 }
	}

					1031 = { add_manpower = 2500 }
				}

				}

				}
				JAP_check_numbers_of_jews_effect = yes
			}

				limit = { 
					check_variable = { JAP_plan_fugu_categ_var = 1 }

				add_to_variable = { JAP_amount_of_jews = 10000 }
				if = { 
					limit = { has_country_flag = JAP_jews_in_shanghai } 
					1145 = { add_manpower = 5000 }
					1031 = { add_manpower = 5000 }
				}

				}

				}
				JAP_check_numbers_of_jews_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { JAP_plan_fugu_categ_var = 2 } 
				}
				add_to_variable = { JAP_amount_of_jews = 20000 }
				if = {
